# 🎯 Elite Behavioral Patterns Report — By Specific Team Name

**Data Range:** Thu Apr 16 2026 to Thu Apr 23 2026

For each scoreline, this report shows which **specific teams** were involved and what happens
to each of those teams in their **very next match**, with a minimum 80% probability.

- **Home Team**: the team that played at HOME when that score occurred
- **Away Team**: the team that played AWAY when that score occurred

> **Minimum sample size per team: 3 matches · Minimum probability: 80%**
